  259: function replaceTemplatePlaceholders(value: string, replacements: Record<string, string>) {

  260:   return String(value ?? "").replace(/\$([a-zA-Z0-9_]+)/g, (match) => {
  261:     const replacement = replacements[match]
  262:     if (replacement === undefined || replacement === null) return match
  263:     const text = String(replacement)
  264:     return text.trim() ? text : match
  265:   })
  266: }
  267:
  268: function templateBodyToHtml(value: string) {
  269:   if (/<[^>]+>/.test(value)) return value
  270:   const lines = value.split(/\r?\n/)
  271:   if (lines.length === 0) return "<p></p>"
  272:   return lines
  273:     .map((line) => {
  274:       const trimmed = line.trim()
  275:       return trimmed ? `<p>${escapeHtml(trimmed)}</p>` : "<p></p>"
  276:     })
  277:     .join("")
  278: }

  118: async function withTimeout<T>(promise: Promise<T>) {
  119:   return Promise.race([
  120:     promise,
  121:     new Promise<T>((_, reject) => setTimeout(() => reject(new Error("Tempo limite da triagem atingido. Pode tentar executar novamente.")), JOB_TIMEOUT_MS)),
  122:   ])
  123: }
  124:
  125: async function execute(nextRunAt?: string) {
  126:   try {
  127:     await setProcessingMessage("Processando e-mails novos na INBOX")
  128:     const result = await withTimeout(processUnreadEmailTriageV2(5000))
  129:     const processed = Number(result.processed || 0)
  130:     const message = result.ok ? `${processed} e-mail(s) processado(s)` : (result.error || "Falha ao processar e-mails")
  131:     await setFinished(Boolean(result.ok), message, processed, nextRunAt, result)
  132:   } catch (error) {
  133:     await setFinished(false, error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error), 0, nextRunAt)
  134:   } finally {
  135:     globalThis.__sigajusEmailTriageJobRunning = false
  136:   }
  137: }
  138:

--- keyword: email / linha 140 ---
  130:     const message = result.ok ? `${processed} e-mail(s) processado(s)` : (result.error || "Falha ao processar e-mails")
  131:     await setFinished(Boolean(result.ok), message, processed, nextRunAt, result)
  132:   } catch (error) {
  133:     await setFinished(false, error instanceof Error ? error.message : String(error), 0, nextRunAt)
  134:   } finally {

  201: async function matchRule(subject: string, body: string, classifier: string): Promise<RuleMatch> {
  202:   const rows = await prisma.$queryRawUnsafe<Array<{ id: string; nome: string; palavras: unknown }>>(`
  203:     SELECT id::text AS id, nome, palavras_chave AS palavras
  204:     FROM public.judicial_email_regras
  205:     WHERE ativo = TRUE
  206:     ORDER BY ordem ASC, nome ASC
  207:   `)
  208:   const haystack = normalizeSearch([subject, body, classifier].join(" \n "))
  209:   for (const row of rows) {
  210:     const palavras = Array.isArray(row.palavras) ? row.palavras.map(text).filter(Boolean) : []
  211:     if (palavras.some((palavra) => haystack.includes(normalizeSearch(palavra)))) {
  212:       const users = await prisma.$queryRawUnsafe<Array<{ id: string; nome: string; email: string }>>(`
  213:         SELECT usuario_id AS id, usuario_nome AS nome, COALESCE(usuario_email, '') AS email
  214:         FROM public.judicial_email_regra_usuarios

--- keyword: attachments / linha 224 ---
  214:         FROM public.judicial_email_regra_usuarios
  215:         WHERE regra_id = $1::bigint AND ativo = TRUE
  216:         ORDER BY usuario_nome ASC
  217:       `, row.id)
  218:       return { id: row.id, nome: text(row.nome), palavras, users: users.map((u) => ({ id: text(u.id), nome: text(u.nome), email: text(u.email).toLowerCase() })) }
  219:     }
  220:   }
  221:   return { id: null, nome: classifier || "NÃ£o classificado", palavras: [], users: [] }
  222: }
  223:
  224: async function saveAttachments(params: { attachments: ParsedAttachment[]; protocolo: string; demandaId?: string | null; emailProcessadoId?: string | null }) {
  225:   const protocoloSeguro = sanitizeSegment(params.protocolo || "email")
  226:   const pastaRelativa = path.posix.join("/uploads", "email-triagem", protocoloSeguro)
  227:   const pastaFisica = path.join(process.cwd(), "public", "uploads", "email-triagem", protocoloSeguro)
  228:   await mkdir(pastaFisica, { recursive: true })
  229:   const saved = []
  230:   for (const attachment of params.attachments || []) {
  231:     const originalName = text(attachment.filename) || "anexo"
  232:     const storedName = `${Date.now()}_${randomUUID().replace(/-/g, "")}_${sanitizeSegment(originalName)}`
  233:     const relativePath = path.posix.join(pastaRelativa, storedName)
  234:     const physicalPath = path.join(pastaFisica, storedName)

  196: function senderText(mail: ParsedMailLike) {
  197:   const first = mail.from?.value?.[0]
  198:   if (first?.address) return [first.name, first.address].map(text).filter(Boolean).join(" <") + (first.name ? ">" : "")
  199:   return text(mail.from?.text)
